7V13H13V7H11Z"></path></svg></span><span class="prose min-w-0 w-full text-amber-900 dark:text-amber-200" data-component-part="callout-content"><p>This endpoint is in <strong>beta</strong> and is subject to change.</p></span></span>
<p>This endpoint is ideal if you have an existing system that generates X12 EDI files and you want to send them through Stedi&#x27;s API.</p>
<ol>
<li>Call this endpoint with a payload in <a href="https://portal.stedi.com/app/guides/view/hipaa/patient-information-x210/01HQ4HZ8ZBY2CZGPCVVM8JTK22" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">275 X12 EDI format</a>.</li>
<li>Stedi sends the attachment to the payer, so the payer can use it to adjudicate the referenced 837 professional, dental, or institutional claim.</li>
<li>The endpoint returns summary information about the attachment submission.</li>
</ol>
<p>This endpoint only supports <a href="/docs/healthcare/submit-claim-attachments#solicited-vs-unsolicited-attachments">unsolicited attachments</a>.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 group" id="size-limit"><a class="peer relative" data-card="" href="#size-limit"><span aria-label="Copy link to section" class="absolute opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all duration-200 p-1 rounded bg-primary hover:bg-secondary dark:bg-neutral-800 dark:hover:bg-neutral-700 border border-neutral-300 dark:border-neutral-600 -left-[28px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 absolute transition-transform"><path d="M18.3638 15.5355L16.9496 14.1213L18.3638 12.7071C20.3164 10.7545 20.3164 7.58866 18.3638 5.63604C16.4112 3.68341 13.2453 3.68341 11.2927 5.63604L9.87849 7.05025L8.46428 5.63604L9.87849 4.22182C12.6122 1.48815 17.0443 1.48815 19.778 4.22182C22.5117 6.95549 22.5117 11.3876 19.778 14.1213L18.3638 15.5355ZM15.5353 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113 5.63585 18.364C7.58847 20.3166 10.7543 20.3166 12.7069 18.364L14.1211 16.9497L15.5353 18.364ZM14.8282 7.75736L16.2425 9.17157L9.17139 16.2426L7.75717 14.8284L14.8282 7.75736Z"></path></svg></span>Size limit</a></h2>
<p>The size limit for attachments submitted in a single request is 6MB. If you need to submit larger attachments, you must submit them through <a href="/docs/healthcare/submit-claims-sftp-connection">Stedi SFTP</a> or the <a href="/docs/healthcare/api-reference/post-healthcare-create-claim-attachment">JSON endpoints</a>.</p><div class="flex items-end justify-between gap-2"><h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center dark:border-neutral-600 -left-[28px] top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 inline-flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon fill-neutral-500 dark:fill-neutral-400 transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M9.9997 15.1709L19.1921 5.97852L20.6063 7.39273L9.9997 17.9993L3.63574 11.6354L5.04996 10.2212L9.9997 15.1709Z"></path></svg><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon 18.364L14.1211 19.7782C11.3875 22.5118 6.95531 22.5118 4.22164 19.7782C1.48797 17.0445 1.48797 12.6123 4.22164 9.87868L5.63585 8.46446L7.05007 9.87868L5.63585 11.2929C3.68323 13.2455 3.68323 16.4113
